# Annual Report — The Synthetic Enterprise

## Executive Summary

This report covers 2016–2025 (10 calendar years,
the last partial). The business survived the full window.

- Starting treasury: £21,829.17
- Final treasury: £48,608.72
  (£26,779.56 net change)
- Gross margin: £45,417.31
- Capital costs: £18,637.75
- Net margin: £26,779.56
- Capital cost ratio: 41.0% of gross
- Risk committee (Context Handshake) interventions: 130
- Bills issued: 1101, average clarity 0.918,
  service quality score 0.935
- Enterprise value (CLV sum across 6 billing accounts): £32,018.72
- Cost to serve (whole portfolio): £6,189.28, net margin after cost to serve: £39,228.03
- Hedge effectiveness (whole window): hedging cost £6,696.63 vs. a fully unhedged book (actual net £26,779.56 vs. naked net £33,476.19)

- **2021** (crisis year): net margin £-1,096.43, 15 risk committee wake-up(s).
- **2022** (crisis year): net margin £4,165.00, 30 risk committee wake-up(s).

## Hedge Effectiveness — Whole Run

This is the most strategically interesting question in the whole
simulation: did the risk committee's hedging interventions actually make
money, or just reduce variance?

- hedging cost £6,696.63 vs. a fully unhedged book (actual net £26,779.56 vs. naked net £33,476.19)
- **Best hedging decision of the run**: C6, term starting
  2021-03-31 (hedge fraction 0.40) -- hedging
  protected £704.57 vs. going naked.
- **Worst hedging decision of the run**: C4g, term
  starting 2022-09-30 (hedge fraction 0.70) --
  over-hedging cost £2,005.47 vs. going
  naked.
